 When i made up my mind to write Yash Chopra for the first time in 1996, many people in India asked me that when there are many and equally interesting figures present in the film industry, why then? The question arose because Yash Chopra's career spans many stages and there is a lot of gaps between them
 is daur main jis nae kism ke ‘bollywood’ cinema kaa unhone aagaaj kiya tha, vah abhi ubhar hi rahaa tha
 Yashji's life and the scope of his work spans from the 50s to today's new globalizing India, which is the entire history of the development of Hindi cinema
 unki filmein in chah dashakon ke dauraan bhartiya samaaj kii pariklpana kaa ek laajawab najariya pesh karti hai
 Like all Hindu Punjabis, Yashji grew up in eastern and western Punjab
 unka janm lahore main hua jahaan unhone urdu or hindi sikhi
 He then moved to Doaba College, Jalandhar
 vibhaajan ke baad yashji ke bade bhai bi
 R
 chopra apane parivaar ko lekar mumbai aa gaye
 In 1952, Yashji also came to Mumbai and never returned to Punjab, but he was not cut off from the roots
 ek aadhunik punjabi hameshaa unki filmon main pramukhataa se rahaa, jo khushmijaaj, jajbaati or utsaahi charitra hua karata tha
 The Punjabi women of his films were also like men, be it from Punjab, Delhi or London
 cinema kaa shuruaati prashikshan yashji ne bi
 R
 chopra se ek sahyogi ke taur par liya, jinaki filmein saamaajik prashnon par kendrit hoti thim, jaise vidhwaa punarvivaah par bani ek hi rasta (1956), audyogikaran par bani nayaa daur (1957) or maut kii sajaa par bani kanoon (1960)
 During this time Yashji learned the story of the film, its style, the importance of the music, the cast of the stars and the characteristics of working with a closely connected production team
 dashakon tak unhone apni ek team ke saath kaam kiya or unheen main se kaiyon ko unhone apane daaen haath ke rup main taiyaar kiya
 Sahir Ludhianvi was also one of them
 vibhaajan ke baad jo hissaa pakistan main chalaa gaya, vahiin se raaj kapur bhi aate the
 In the 50s, Raj Kapoor created the image of a new romantic hero
 yashji par isane gahari chhap chodi
 Raj Kapoor, who was just eight years older than Yashji, was his mentor and inspiration and this can be seen clearly in Yash Chopra's style, whether 'his heroine draped in white clothes' or Punjabi tunes music introduced in modern way , Which became quite popular
 bi
 R
 chopra or raaj kapur ne bhartiya film udyog kaa punjabikaran kar diya
 The series began in the 40s with Punjabi becoming a trend in Punjabi music, costumes and even language
 yashji kii shuruaati filmein biaar films ke binar tale baniin: dhul kaa phool (1959) ek avivaahit maa kii kahani thi jisamen pita ko uski jimmedaari na nibhaane ke liye dandit kiya jaataa he
 In the context of hindu-muslim unity, a song of the film became very famous: "you will become a Hindu, you will become a Muslim, a human being is a human being
 ’’ yashji kii duusari film dharmaputra (1961) main 1925 ke baad ke hindu-muslim sambandhon kaa khaakaa khinchaa gaya he
 Time in 1965 is also a memorable film that first established the style, set and lifestyle of the modern urban Indian youth
 multistar filmon main bhi yah shuruaati thi
 There is also a mention of Partition, which is depicted as an earthquake in which the family of Lala Kedarnath is shattered
 film kaa kendriya vichaar yah he ki hamaara apni niyati par koi vash nahin
 We should accept whatever comes out in life
 yah baat film ke mashhoor geet ‘‘aage bhi jane naa tu’’ main kahi gai he

 aar
 Yash Chopra opened his production house under the name Yash Raj Films after making two more films with (man Aur Insaan and Ittefaq in 1969) and made his first film Daag in 1973
 yahi vah dashak tha jab yash chopra ne amitabh bachchan ke saath milakar kaam karnaa shuru kiya or do tarah kii filmein unhen lekar banaain
 There was a series of films in which Amitabh's character is named Vijay
 inaki script saleem-javed kii thi
 In these films, there is a child with injustice done in childhood and he grows up to avenge the injustice done to his family
 1975 main bani diwaar main yah ninsaphi baahar ke logon ne kii thi to 1978 main ai trishul main ek garbhvatee mahila ke saath ninsaphi uske purush mitra ne kii thi
 The second type of films made about Amitabh are named as "amitya" category films in which Bachchan plays the role of a romantic hero
 isamen nayak apane prem ke liye samaaj ke saath sangharsh main utarataa he lekin baad main use abhas hota he ki asli pyaar to paaramparik paariwarik dhaanche ke bheetar hi mil saktaa he
 Kabhi Kabhi (1976) and Silsila (1981) are representative films of this theme
 kabhi kabhi main avivaahit maataaon, baccha god lene tathaa bacchon or maa-baap ke rishte ke muddon ko uthaaya gaya he jabaki silsilaa main bichade hue premi yugal kii kahani he jo apni shaadi ke baad dobaaraa ek hona chaahate hai par unhen ahsaas hota he ki apane nae jivan ke hisaab se hi unhen khud ko dhaalnaa hoga
 The films made by Yashji in the eighties were somewhat less successful
 inamen ek yaadgaar film thi mashaal (1984) jo mumbai kii patrakarita or sangathit aparaadh par aadhaarit he
 In this, a senior journalist becomes a mafia after the injustice done to him, while a younger journalist fights crime successfully using the media
 1985 main bani faasale ko sirf isliye yaad rakhaa jaataa he kyonki yah pehali film thi jise yashji ne switzraland main shoot kiya tha
 In 1989, Yash Chopra regained her top position by making Chandni and her romantic brand was restored
 1993 main unhone shahrukh khan ko lekar dar banaai or isse kahin zyada vivaadaaspad film lamhe 1991 main banaai jo unki pehali gaiyr-punjabi film kahi ja sakati he
 The credit for resurrecting Yash Raj's style goes to his son Aditya Chopra, who will take Dilwale Dulhania in 1995 and in 1997 inspired Dil To Pagal Hai
 in donon filmon ne nae bharat kii nabj ko pakadaa tha jo parampara ko chode bagaiyr aadhunik or upabhoktavaadi bhi bananaa chaah rahaa tha
 Yash Chopra was a complex man as a person
 adhiktar logon ke saamne inkaa cheharaa ek filmkaar, nirmaataa, kathakaar, safal kaarobaari or profeshnal kaa he
 His personality had another face which would have been quiet in private, and Punjabi looked enthusiastic and present among the family
 ek prabhaavshaalee kaarobaari lekin ek sahaj or vinamr madhyavargeey pariwari aadmi
 He was tough as a businessman but very soft towards his loved ones
 ve kehete the, ‘‘main ek imotional buddhu hum
 "yashji may not be at work, but the sense of duty within him was tremendous
" film banane ke alaava ve kisi or cheez se yadi utana hi khush hote to vah tha khaane par dost-mitron or parijanon kaa jamaavada
 The formula of his life was, "family, film and food
 ’’ unki duniya ke centre main thim unki patni pamela, jo unki takat thim
 His relationship with his sons was very close and strong
 yashji acha insaan bananaa chaahate the or mujhase aksar poochhate bhi the ki kya main vaisaa hum? kaash! main unhen bataa paati ki ve ek mahaan shaks the or unhen apane mitra ke rup main paakar mujhe bahut garv he
